# Graph Report - workspace  (2026-07-11)

## Corpus Check
- 1593 files · ~3,525,463 words
- Verdict: corpus is large enough that graph structure adds value.

## Summary
- 20218 nodes · 26675 edges · 1950 communities (1432 shown, 518 thin omitted)
- Extraction: 90% EXTRACTED · 10% INFERRED · 0% AMBIGUOUS · INFERRED: 2776 edges (avg confidence: 0.78)
- Token cost: 0 input · 0 output

## Graph Freshness
- Built from commit: `05b5f70b`
- Run `git rev-parse HEAD` and compare to check if the graph is stale.
- Run `graphify update .` after code changes (no API cost).
